  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=8.2)
    The plot progresses with remarkable coherence despite its ambitious scope. The journey from garage sale discovery to pyramid exploration to transformation unfolds logically, with the envelope serving as an elegant plot device. The story achieves a satisfying arc with clear causality between Marcus's unique qualification and his ultimate purpose. The only weakness is the somewhat convenient placement of the envelope, which borders on contrivance but ultimately serves the narrative's deeper themes.

  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=7.9)
    Plot progresses logically through Morrow's negotiation attempt, but the leap to handshaking the Leviathan feels underdeveloped; connections between naptime setting and climax are underexploited despite strong conceptual irony.

  * grade_story_101.txt (grade=6.1)
    Abstract progression lacks concrete action or stakes, but achieves thematic resonance through cyclical, meditative structure. Resolution feels preordained rather than earned.

  * grade_story_10.txt (grade=8.0)
    Story maintains coherence through its narrow timeframe but struggles with compressed emotional shifts. The revelation in the chest serves as a structural anchor, though the pivot from vengeance to forgiveness occurs without visceral dramatization of the decision-making process.

  * grade_story_100.txt (grade=6.8)
    Moon paths and penny collecting drive circular meditation on cosmic deception rather than a traditional plot. Coherence exists through imagery rather than narrative progression; constrained word count benefits atmospheric density but weakens dramatic tension.

  * grade_story_102.txt (grade=6.5)
    Plot hinges on prophecy fulfillment, but the pivotal key-turning lacks tangible stakes or preparation. The tight word limit results in abrupt thematic shifts, sacrificing momentum for concept.

  * grade_story_112.txt (grade=8.2)
    Plot mechanics work but feel contrived—hopscotch board as key lacks organic integration with Nüshu’s cultural context.

  * grade_story_104.txt (grade=7.4)
    Modifications drive plot but timeline compression strains believability. The orchard framing bookends effectively, though the brief transformation feels underexplored despite word constraints.

  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=7.4)
    Tightly paced narrative connects garage sale to pyramid, though descent into pyramid feels compressed. Method (unraveling knots) drives plot effectively, but resolution of claustrophobia during descent lacks sufficient payoff.

  * grade_story_103.txt (grade=8.1)
    High tension between truth and illusion drives the plot, but the transition from contemplation to decision feels abrupt. The mirrored moment’s ephemeral nature isn’t fully interrogated, slightly undermining coherence.

  * grade_story_108.txt (grade=7.4)
    Plot structure demonstrates admirable compression, with cause-effect chain from pen activation to crowd control. However, the "tapestry of fate" framing feels tacked-on rather than organically connected to the immediate action and conceptual payoff.

  * grade_story_111.txt (grade=9.1)
